## Accordion

### CreateAccordionProps`<Multiple>`

#### Type parameters

▪ **Multiple** extends `boolean` = `false`

#### Properties

##### defaultValue

> **defaultValue**?: `WhenTrue`\<`Multiple`, `string`[], `string`, `string` \| `string`[]\>

The uncontrolled default value of the accordion.

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:45](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L45)

##### disabled

> **disabled**?: `boolean`

When `true`, prevents the user from interacting with the accordion.

###### Default

```ts
false
```

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:30](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L30)

##### forceVisible

> **forceVisible**?: `boolean`

Whether the accordion content should be displayed even if it is not open.
This is useful for animating the content in and out using transitions.

###### See

https://melt-ui.com/docs/transitions

###### Default

```ts
false
```

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:40](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L40)

##### multiple

> **multiple**?: `Multiple`

If `true`, multiple accordion items can be open at the same time.

###### Default

```ts
false
```

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:23](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L23)

##### onValueChange

> **onValueChange**?: `ChangeFn`\<`undefined` \| `WhenTrue`\<`Multiple`, `string`[], `string`, `string` \| `string`[]\>\>

A callback called when the value of the `value` store should be changed.

###### See

https://melt-ui.com/docs/controlled#change-functions

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:60](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L60)

##### value

> **value**?: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `WhenTrue`\<`Multiple`, `string`[], `string`, `string` \| `string`[]\>\>

The controlled value store for the accordion.
If provided, this will override the value passed to `defaultValue`.

###### See

https://melt-ui.com/docs/controlled#bring-your-own-store

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts:53](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/accordion/types.ts#L53)

***

### Accordion`<Multiple>`

> **Accordion**\<`Multiple`\>: `BuilderReturn`\<*typeof* [`createAccordion`](exports.md#createaccordion)\>

#### Type parameters

| Parameter | Default |
| :------ | :------ |

### ComboboxSelected`<Multiple, Value>`

> **ComboboxSelected**\<`Multiple`, `Value`\>: `WhenTrue`\<`Multiple`, [`ComboboxOption`](exports.md#comboboxoptionvalue)\<`Value`\>[], [`ComboboxOption`](exports.md#comboboxoptionvalue)\<`Value`\>\>

### Select`<Value, Multiple, S>`

> **Select**\<`Value`, `Multiple`, `S`\>: `BuilderReturn`\<*typeof* [`createSelect`](exports.md#createselect)\>

#### Type parameters

| Parameter | Default |
| :------ | :------ |
| `Value` | `unknown` |
| `Multiple` extends `boolean` | `false` |

Creates an ARIA-1.2-compliant combobox.

#### Type parameters

▪ **Value**

▪ **Multiple** extends `boolean` = `false`

▪ **S** extends [`ComboboxOption`](exports.md#comboboxoptionvalue)\<`Value`\>[] \| [`ComboboxOption`](exports.md#comboboxoptionvalue)\<`Value`\> = [`ComboboxSelected`](exports.md#comboboxselectedmultiple-value)\<`Multiple`, `Value`\>

#### Parameters

▪ **props?**: [`CreateComboboxProps`](exports.md#createcomboboxpropsvalue-multiple-s)\<`Value`, `Multiple`, `S`\>

> 8
> ```

>

> the escape key.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> true
> ```
>
> ##### options.closeOnOutsideClick
>
> > **options.closeOnOutsideClick**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `true`
>

> outside of the listbox.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> true
> ```
>
> ##### options.defaultSelected
>
> > **options.defaultSelected**?: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `S`\>
>

>

>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> undefined
> ```
>

>
> > **options.disabled**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `false`

>
> > **options.forceVisible**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `false`
>

> This is useful for animating the content in and out using transitions.
>
> ###### See
>
> https://melt-ui.com/docs/transitions
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> false
> ```
>

### createDialog()

> **createDialog**(`props`?): \{
  `elements`: \{
     `close`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<`undefined` \| `Stores`, (`node`) => `MeltActionReturn`\<`"click"` \| `"keydown"`\>, () => \{
        `type`: `"button"`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `content`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<[`Readable`\<`boolean`\>], (`node`) => \{
        `destroy`: (...`args`) => `void`;
        }, (`__namedParameters`) => \{
        `aria-describedby`: `string`;
        `aria-labelledby`: `string`;
        `data-state`: `string`;
        `hidden`: `undefined` \| `boolean`;
        `id`: `string`;
        `role`: `"dialog"` \| `"alertdialog"`;
        `style`: `string`;
        `tabindex`: `number`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `description`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<`undefined` \| `Stores`, `Action`\<`any`, `any`, `Record`\<`never`, `any`\>\>, () => \{
        `id`: `string`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `overlay`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<[`Readable`\<`boolean`\>], \<`Node`\>(`node`) => \{
        `destroy`: `void`;
        }, (`__namedParameters`) => \{
        `aria-hidden`: `true`;
        `data-state`: `"open"` \| `"closed"`;
        `hidden`: `undefined` \| `true`;
        `style`: `string`;
        `tabindex`: `-1`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `portalled`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<`Writable`\<`null` \| `string` \| `HTMLElement`\>, \<`Node`\>(`node`) => \{
        `destroy`: `void`;
        }, (`$portal`) => \{
        `data-portal`: `undefined` \| `string`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `title`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<`undefined` \| `Stores`, `Action`\<`any`, `any`, `Record`\<`never`, `any`\>\>, () => \{
        `id`: `string`;
     }, `string`\>;
     `trigger`: `ExplicitBuilderReturn`\<\{
        `set`: (`this`, `value`) => `void`;
        `update`: (`updater`, `sideEffect`?) => `void`;
        `subscribe`: `Unsubscriber`;
        }, (`node`) => `MeltActionReturn`\<`"click"` \| `"keydown"`\>, (`$open`) => \{
        `aria-controls`: `string`;
        `aria-expanded`: `boolean`;
        `aria-haspopup`: `"dialog"`;
        `id`: `string`;
        `type`: `"button"`;
     }, `string`\>;
  };
  `ids`: \{
     `content`: `string`;
     `description`: `string`;
     `title`: `string`;
     `trigger`: `string`;
  };
  `options`: \{
     `closeOnEscape`: `Writable`\<`boolean`\>;
     `closeOnOutsideClick`: `Writable`\<`boolean`\>;
     `defaultOpen`: `Writable`\<`boolean`\>;
     `forceVisible`: `Writable`\<`boolean`\>;
     `onOpenChange`: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `ChangeFn`\<`boolean`\>\>;
     `open`: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `Writable`\<`boolean`\>\>;
     `portal`: `Writable`\<`null` \| `string` \| `HTMLElement`\>;
     `preventScroll`: `Writable`\<`boolean`\>;
     `role`: `Writable`\<`"dialog"` \| `"alertdialog"`\>;
  };
  `states`: \{
     `open`: \{
        `set`: (`this`, `value`) => `void`;
        `update`: (`updater`, `sideEffect`?) => `void`;
        `subscribe`: `Unsubscriber`;
     };
  };
}

> ##### options.defaultOpen
>
> > **options.defaultOpen**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `false`
>

>

>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> false
> ```
>

>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> 'ltr'
> ```
>
> ##### options.forceVisible
>
> > **options.forceVisible**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `false`
>
> Whether the menu content should be displayed even if it is not open.
> This is useful for animating the content in and out using transitions.
>
> ###### See
>
> https://melt-ui.com/docs/transitions
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> false
> ```
>
> ##### options.loop
>
> > **options.loop**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `false`
>
> Whether or not to loop the menu navigation.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> false
> ```
>
> ##### options.onOpenChange
>
> > **options.onOpenChange**?: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `ChangeFn`\<`boolean`\>\>
>
> A callback for when the open state changes.
>
> ###### See
>
> https://melt-ui.com/docs/controlled#change-functions
>
> ##### options.open
>
> > **options.open**?: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `Writable`\<`boolean`\>\>
>
> A controlled open state store for the menu. If provided, the
> value of this store will override the `defaultOpen` prop.
>
> ###### See
>
> https://melt-ui.com/docs/controlled#bring-your-own-store
>
> ##### options.portal
>
> > **options.portal**: `Writable`\<`undefined` \| `null` \| `string` \| `HTMLElement`\> = `undefined`
>
> If not `undefined`, the menu will be rendered within the provided element or selector.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> 'body'
> ```
>
> ##### options.positioning
>
> > **options.positioning**: `Writable`\<`FloatingConfig` \| \{
> `placement`: `"bottom"`;
> }\>
>
> Options for positioning the popover menu.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> placement: 'bottom'
> ```
>
> ##### options.preventScroll
>
> > **options.preventScroll**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `true`
>
> Whether or not to prevent scrolling when the menu is open.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> true
> ```
>
> ##### options.typeahead
>
> > **options.typeahead**: `Writable`\<`boolean`\> = `true`
>
> Whether to use typeahead to automatically focus elements.
>
> ###### Default
>
> ```ts
> true
> ```

> ```

> ```

  `elements`: \{

>
> If set to `true`, whenever you open this tooltip, all other tooltips
> with `group` also set to `true` will close. If you pass in a string
> instead, only tooltips with the same `group` value will be closed.

### melt()

> **melt**\<`Builder`, `Element`, `Attributes`, `A`, `Param`\>(`node`, `params`): `ActionReturn`\<`Builder`, `Attributes`\>

A special action for Melt UI's preprocessor `@melt-ui/pp`.

#### Type parameters

▪ **Builder** extends `SomeBuilder`\<`Element`, `Param`, `A`\>

▪ **Element** extends `HTMLElement`

▪ **Attributes** extends `Record`\<`string`, `any`\>

▪ **A** extends `Record`\<`string`, `any`\>

▪ **Param** = `never`

#### Parameters

▪ **node**: `Element`

▪ **params**: `Builder`

#### Returns

#### See

https://www.melt-ui.com/docs/preprocessor

#### Example

```svelte
<script>
	import { createLabel, melt } from '@melt-ui/svelte';
	const { elements: { root } } = createLabel();
</script>

<label use:melt={$root} />
```

#### Source

[src/lib/internal/actions/melt/index.ts:29](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/internal/actions/melt/index.ts#L29)

### CreateTableOfContentsProps

Arguments to be passed to the Table of Contents builder.

#### Type Param

The id of the container in which the content of the page is.

#### Param

A list of headings that should be excluded in the table.

#### Param

The pixel offset that should be added when scrolling to a heading.

#### Param

Describes whether the scroll behaviour should be smooth or not.

#### Param

Describes which headings should be considered active.

##### activeType

> **activeType**?: [`ActiveType`](exports.md#activetype-1)

## TableOfContents

### CreateTableOfContentsProps

Arguments to be passed to the Table of Contents builder.

#### Type Param

The id of the container in which the content of the page is.

#### Param

A list of headings that should be excluded in the table.

#### Param

The pixel offset that should be added when scrolling to a heading.

#### Param

Describes whether the scroll behaviour should be smooth or not.

#### Param

Describes which headings should be considered active.

##### group

> **group**?: `string` \| `boolean`

If set to `true`, whenever you open this tooltip, all other tooltips
with `group` also set to `true` will close. If you pass in a string
instead, only tooltips with the same `group` value will be closed.

###### Source

[src/lib/builders/tooltip/types.ts:30](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/tooltip/types.ts#L30)

##### expanded

> **expanded**?: `Writable`\<`string`[]\>

Optionally pass a writable store to control the expanded items of the tree.
If provided, this will override the value of the `defaultTree` prop.

###### See

https://melt-ui.com/docs/controlled#bring-your-own-store

[src/lib/builders/tree/types.ts:26](https://github.com/huntabyte/melt-ui/blob/7f902e45/src/lib/builders/tree/types.ts#L26)
